name:Hâ€eâ€yâ€oâ€uâ€tâ€iâ€aâ€nâ€xâ€iâ€a
info:Guestroom - Garden-View (Double bed) (East building)
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Family
info:15 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted March 14, 2024
msg:Xinzhi Hotel is located at No. 215, Yongfeng West Road, Haishu District, Ningbo. It was once the state guesthouse of Ningbo and is almost a household name.

The hotel has four main buildings in the east, west, south and north. The three buildings in the east, west and north are guest rooms. The front desk is in the east building, and the restaurant is in the west building, which are connected by a corridor. The south building is a sports and fitness building.
I stayed in the east building last night. The guest room was clean and tidy, the space was large enough, and the staff was polite.
The most impressive thing is: the buffet breakfast is rich in variety, and the more distinctive ones are freshly baked sesame biscuits, cappuccino and other freshly ground coffees. For the standard 48 yuan buffet breakfast, it is really worth the money, which is higher than the high-star hotels of the same standard.
The self-operated swimming pool has clear water quality and a pool length of 25 meters. Among all the high-star hotels in Ningbo, it feels that it should be ranked in the top three.
The only drawback is that the locker room is a bit small.
----------------------------------------

msg:We traveled to Ningbo with four elderly and one child. The hotel's swimming pool was a highlight. We swam three times in three days and two nights. The sports hall was great. The hotel is located in the city center, but the garden design makes the hotel quiet in the bustling city. It is also very convenient to eat. You can reach well-known large shopping malls in about ten minutes by car. The accommodation is on the first floor. The air conditioner is turned to the maximum at night, but it is still cold. The room service provided heaters for all three of our rooms, which immediately made us feel very warm. The manager of the breakfast restaurant was amiable. Seeing that we brought children, he personally heated up the steamed buns and sent them to the table. The meals were clean and hygienic, with a variety of varieties. There was also a grand piano next to the room for the elderly to play and entertain. If you forget your belongings in the hotel after leaving, the staff will take the initiative to contact the courier to your home. The service is perfect. I hope it will get better and better in the future!

msg:The location is very good. Although the subway is being built at the door, it is in a good location in the old city. The attractions in the city are all within 3 or 4 kilometers. It costs about 10 yuan to take a taxi. The subway entrance is 20 meters away from the door.

The yard is beautiful, the garden is elegant and tasteful, the ecological environment is also very good, there are many happy birds singing, and a river flows quietly next to it. It is very pleasant to take parents and children for a walk.

The room is spacious and elegant, with a view outside each window. The room is also very clean. Although it is on the first floor, it has dehumidification + air conditioning, dry and warm, and the bedding is also very comfortable. It is particularly worth praising that there are many details. The night lights and bathroom sensor lights, as well as mirrors and towel racks are better than luxury hotels.

Although the breakfast room is not big, the breakfast is rich in variety, high quality and good taste.

The service is also full marks. Every staff member I met when checking in was gentle, polite and considerate. We stayed calmly and happily. Recently, I like to choose such a high-quality state-owned hotel when traveling with parents and children. It is generally in a good location in the city. Compared with other hotels, it has an advantage in the environment, hardware is guaranteed, and good service is perfect. The Qisheng International Hotel I stayed at when I went to Zibo was also very good. You can see the Haidai Building and the Convention and Exhibition Center from the room.
